  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_92b23694-9d44-4cc0-8745-61a98d040552'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initializeSiwa();

  <span id="freeText18237681900403885121" style="display:none"><i>“Life is full of crossroads, Alex. Full of choices.”</i><br /><br />Returning for a second year at Akarnae Academy with her gifted friends, Alexandra Jennings steps back through a doorway into Medora, the fantasy world that is full of impossibilities. <br /><br />Despite the magical wonder of Medora, Alex’s life remains threatened by Aven Dalmarta, the banished prince from the Lost City of Meya who is out for her blood. <br /><br />To protect the Medorans from Aven’s quest to reclaim his birthright, Alex and her friends seek out the Meyarin city and what remains of its ancient race.<br /><br />Not sure who—or perhaps <i>what</i>—she is anymore, all Alex knows is that if she fails to keep Aven from reaching Meya, the lives of countless Medorans will be in danger. Can she protect them, or will all be lost?</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18989854-krystal?shelf=aussie-authors">aussie-authors</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1841687518" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer255363294997210557">**Re-read Jan/Feb 19**<br/><br/><b>MY HEART.</b><br/><br/>This is definitely the book that hooked me firmly on the series.<br/><br/><i>The escapades.<br/><br/>The characters.<br/><br/><b>THE DRAMA.</b></i><br/><br/>And yet still so much sass.<br/><br/>Where's those handy check marks ...<br/><br/>✓Alex is getting better at fighting<br/>✓Meeting new friends: HELLO Roka and Kyia and Zain and oh hey a cameo from that one guy that we're all definitely falling in love with very soon<br/>✓Spending more time with old friends ie I TOTALLY SHIP ALEX AND KAIDEN THEY ARE ADORABLE<br/>✓More super powers hooray!<br/>✓Teachers t</span>
  <span id="freeText255363294997210557" style="display:none">**Re-read Jan/Feb 19**<br /><br /><b>MY HEART.</b><br /><br />This is definitely the book that hooked me firmly on the series.<br /><br /><i>The escapades.<br /><br />The characters.<br /><br /><b>THE DRAMA.</b></i><br /><br />And yet still so much sass.<br /><br />Where's those handy check marks ...<br /><br />✓Alex is getting better at fighting<br />✓Meeting new friends: HELLO Roka and Kyia and Zain and oh hey a cameo from that one guy that we're all definitely falling in love with very soon<br />✓Spending more time with old friends ie I TOTALLY SHIP ALEX AND KAIDEN THEY ARE ADORABLE<br />✓More super powers hooray!<br />✓Teachers trying to kill students; how very relatable<br />✓The whole SAS trip was SO MUCH FUN<br />✓Alex is so snarky when she lacks sleep which I love, but she's also just naturally a sass queen which means I love her even though everyone else loves her and I'm not usually one to follow trends<br />✓Lots of fighting, I LOVE FIGHT CLUB and mostly just Declan enjoying beating the snot out of Alex and Alex taking it like a champ<br />✓BUT NOT FOR LONG, BUCKO!<br /><br /><i>This concludes my nonsensical babbling inspired by my love of this series which is only growing stronger with re-reads. For sense, please read my original review, below.</i><br /><br />**Original Review**<br /><br /><b>SO GOOD. </b><br /><br />This series is so much better than I expected! The first one was quite obviously Harry Potter-inspired but with this second novel the story has certainly taken on its own life, making it quite an exciting read.<br /><br />There's still way too many good looking people but <b>these characters are so easy to fall for</b> because of the dynamics they bring to the story. I love the friendships and particularly the teamwork, which gives our heroine a great support network instead of the 'only I can do this' complex so many teen fantasy heroes end up with. <br /><br /><b>I love the variety of the classes</b> and the little details that flesh out the world as a place of magic. There's still a few predictable elements and typical scenarios but surprisingly this didn't bother me in the slightest as I truly enjoyed reading through these moments. As with the first novel, there's a few explanations that you can't really think too much about (such as Alex's extremely unconcerned parents) but if you let go of the details and relax into the story you'll find yourself enjoying the ride.<br /><br />Absolutely loved it! Can't wait to get my hands on the next one!<br /><br />***<br /><br />Review for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23569787.Akarnae__The_Medoran_Chronicles___1_" title="Akarnae (The Medoran Chronicles, #1) by Lynette Noni" rel="nofollow noopener">Akarnae</a> (4★s) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1631335573" rel="nofollow noopener">HERE</a><br />Review for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/29570559.Draekora__The_Medoran_Chronicles___3_" title="Draekora (The Medoran Chronicles, #3) by Lynette Noni" rel="nofollow noopener">Draekora</a> (5★s) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1841687530" rel="nofollow noopener">HERE</a><br />Review for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/35439559.Graevale__The_Medoran_Chronicles___4_" title="Graevale (The Medoran Chronicles, #4) by Lynette Noni" rel="nofollow noopener">Graevale</a> (5★s) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2031039032" rel="nofollow noopener">HERE</a><br />Review for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/38459424.We_Three_Heroes__The_Medoran_Chronicles___4_5_" title="We Three Heroes (The Medoran Chronicles, #4.5) by Lynette Noni" rel="nofollow noopener">We Three Heroes</a> (4★s) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2502505830" rel="nofollow noopener">HERE</a><br />Review for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/39808670.Vardaesia__The_Medoran_Chronicles___5_" title="Vardaesia (The Medoran Chronicles, #5) by Lynette Noni" rel="nofollow noopener">Vardaesia</a> (5★s) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2501599563" rel="nofollow noopener">HERE</a></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2337007-brenda?shelf=5000-2020">5000-2020</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2337007-brenda?shelf=sent-by-publisher">sent-by-publisher</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2337007-brenda?shelf=autographed-book">autographed-book</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2757805124" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2834902597700096205">Alexandra Jennings was excited for her second year at Akarnae Academy and rejoining the friends she’d made the previous year. Little did she know the events which would unfold over that year – how much the hated Aven Dalmarta would dominate her thoughts. <br/><br/>As the four friends - Alex, DC, Jordan and Bear - picked up their new timetables for the fourth-year students, Alex was mostly pleased with her schedule. But when she was invited to participate in a trial for another course, she declined. She ha</span>
  <span id="freeText2834902597700096205" style="display:none">Alexandra Jennings was excited for her second year at Akarnae Academy and rejoining the friends she’d made the previous year. Little did she know the events which would unfold over that year – how much the hated Aven Dalmarta would dominate her thoughts. <br /><br />As the four friends - Alex, DC, Jordan and Bear - picked up their new timetables for the fourth-year students, Alex was mostly pleased with her schedule. But when she was invited to participate in a trial for another course, she declined. She had enough on her plate without adding another grueling few hours a week. <br /><br />Coming up with a plan to keep the city of Meya safe; stopping the banished prince who was attempting to return to Meya; Alex knew she’d have to find the Meyarin city if she was to have any success. She had a few tricks up her sleeve, but could she pull it off? The danger was phenomenal, but she knew she had no choice. Alex was determined to stop Aven if it was the last thing she did. At least she had her friends by her side…<br /><br />Wow! What an exceptional read <i>Raelia</i> was! Book 2 in The Medoran Chronicles by Aussie author Lynette Noni, and I devoured it! 448 pages read in a matter of hours; it was that good! Twists, intrigue, magic, fantasy, tough decisions – it was all there. I’m really looking forward to the next – <i>Draekora</i> - soon. Highly recommended.<br /><br />With thanks to Pantera Press for my copy to read in exchange for an honest review.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2834902597700096205" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1938897700" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1938897700" />
    <a title="Ryan Buckby" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/32429909-ryan-buckby"><img alt="Ryan Buckby" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528436487p2/32429909.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1938897700?book_show_action=true">Mar 21, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ryan Buckby" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ryan Buckby" href="/user/show/32429909-ryan-buckby">Ryan Buckby</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1938897700" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10455771621543189122"><b> First read: March 21st 2017 </b><br/><b> Re-read: January 24th 2018, March 6th 2020 </b><br/><br/><b> Life is full of crossroads, Alex. Full of choices </b><br/><br/><br/><b> When day and night combine and fight against one enemy then dark and light shall meet mid-strike and set the captives free </b><br/><br/>Trying to put my emotions in check is going to be extremely hard after finishing this book and boy Lynette has taken this series to a whole new level in this second book and i cannot wait to see where it goes in book three.<br/><br/>This book picks up a couple o</span>
  <span id="freeText10455771621543189122" style="display:none"><b> First read: March 21st 2017 </b><br /><b> Re-read: January 24th 2018, March 6th 2020 </b><br /><br /><b> Life is full of crossroads, Alex. Full of choices </b><br /><br /><br /><b> When day and night combine and fight against one enemy then dark and light shall meet mid-strike and set the captives free </b><br /><br />Trying to put my emotions in check is going to be extremely hard after finishing this book and boy Lynette has taken this series to a whole new level in this second book and i cannot wait to see where it goes in book three.<br /><br />This book picks up a couple of months after the first book and Alex is getting ready to begin her second year at Akarnae. I loved how Alex returned to earth to find a massive search party for her going on because her parents find out that she never enrolled in her school classes. I secretly thought that her parent's knew about Medora and Akarnae and were just keeping it a secret from her but they had no idea of such a place existing. I had a little laugh when Alex told her parents and they were excited at the prospect of having a whole new world to learn and discover just like Alex did in the first book. <br /><br />I loved learning more about Medora and the school in this book and i love how Lynette has handled it because we are learning about these places and things for the first time just like Alex's is and i'm always left wondering if theres anything more to discover and boom Lynette throws more information into the book. It hasn't been information overload either like in most books, you start to find things all throughout the book at different stages and before something big is about to go down. The world that Lynette has created is magical and a place i could see myself living in because there's so much to do and see and learn from. <br /><br />The characters in this book are so well-written and are a group of friends that i want in my own life because they all bring something different to the table. Alex for her determination, fight and loyalty because she never gives up on her family, friends and the challenges she's given. Jordan for his wit, loyalty and sense of humour. Bear for his smarts, loyalty and sense of humour. D.C for her compassion, loyalty, understanding. Friendship plays such a big role in this series because all four of the main characters are so close to each other and it definitely shows and i seriously need these four characters as my friends in real life. <br /><br />There also so many other amazing characters in this series that make it worth reading from when you start the book right up until the end of the book. The stealth and Subterfuge class made up of Kaiden, Blink, Pipsqueak, Skyla Fay and Tom Barrett all of these characters were all amazing and added something to the story in there own right. It was good to see Kaiden return in this one and i'm surprised to see the relationship forming between Alex and himself because i honestly don't see anything myself and i do see something more between Alex and Jordan. <br /><br />But the pairings don't really bother me that much and i love how insta love wasn't a thing in this story because that would have ruined the good thing thats going on right now, i really do like stories that flesh characters out first before they go any further with them. <br /><br />can we all talk about the last few chapters of the book and how much of a shock and devastation that was, I really was feeling what Alex, Bear and D.C were feeling and my heart was breaking for them and i really do hope they can attempt to save Jordan in the next book.. i don't know how or when but i really hope they can. <br /><br />I need Draekora right now but i'm glad the third book is coming out next week so i won't have to long of a wait to continue my adventures with Alex, Jordan, Bear and D.C.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10455771621543189122" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1360833024" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1360833024" />
    <a title="Frannie Pan" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/20502251-frannie-pan"><img alt="Frannie Pan" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1480017050p2/20502251.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1360833024?book_show_action=true">Aug 11, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Frannie Pan" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Frannie Pan" href="/user/show/20502251-frannie-pan">Frannie Pan</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/20502251-frannie-pan?shelf=z-2015">z-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/20502251-frannie-pan?shelf=2016-releases">2016-releases</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1360833024" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5312754891849913286">My God, this book. <br/>I’ve come to love Lynette Noni and her stories like few things in these past couple of months. It is a combination of multiple factors that make her books a second home to me, nothing different from what I would expect from her.<br/>It has become a safe haven where I can go to find comfort and cuddle myself, for I know what will be waiting after I cross the threshold and I can count on a hand’s fingers the rare cases to which this statement also applies. <br/>And please don’t confuse my</span>
  <span id="freeText5312754891849913286" style="display:none">My God, this book. <br />I’ve come to love Lynette Noni and her stories like few things in these past couple of months. It is a combination of multiple factors that make her books a second home to me, nothing different from what I would expect from her.<br />It has become a safe haven where I can go to find comfort and cuddle myself, for I know what will be waiting after I cross the threshold and I can count on a hand’s fingers the rare cases to which this statement also applies. <br />And please don’t confuse my phrasing with predictability or boredom. It would be like saying that Cassandra Clare is predictable and boring with her awesome perfect books. I know, right? Crazy.<br /><br />I can’t really say much about this book, being it the 2nd installment in a series. <br />Alex and her friends are back at Akarnae Academy for another year of getting their asses kicked in combat or getting mixed in the weirdest and most dangerous situations. In fact, they’re not the only ones to be back. After all, Alex is the chosen one by the Library and only she can open the portals to Meya, the ancient place from where Aven was banished and that he’s trying to reach to carry out his revenge. <br /><br />Medora is the same world but so much has changed.<br />The writing style keeps up its lightheartedness, its sarcastic tone and extreme fluency. Seriously, Raelia is 400 pages long and I had an exam coming up but I still read this whole thing in three days and no more. I couldn’t have let go of it even if I had wanted to, I was way too sucked into what was going on. And I didn’t want to let go anyway, so that was ideal. I would describe it as a perfect mix of Jennifer L. Armentrout, for its addicting effect on the reader, and Sarah J. Maas, due to the 100% sure fact you’ll fall in love with more or less the whole male population present in this series. Which is crazy, considering there’s not really a love story yet. My goodness, the tension. It’s eating me alive, I just need something to happen between Alex and… someone! <br />I did miss one character in this installment but it was compensated by tons of other characters’ development and hopefully things will balance out in the sequel.<br />Plus, I must mention those nice addictions to the story that I always go crazy for, such as Alex’s timetable or some notes and messages from professors and so on. I <br />Still waiting for my map but hey, there’s time for it since The Medoran Chronicles is going to be a 5 books series. Yep, you heard me right. 5 books long. It’s Christmas all over again. <br />I mean, after all the shenanigans that went down at the end of Raelia… Lynette Noni was evil. So evil. <br />I just need a bit more of descriptions for it to be absolutely perfect.<br /><br />Where’s book 3? Someone’d better give it to me. And something needs to happen between Alex and this… someone or so help me God!!! <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="5312754891849913286" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText6927524970997339193" style="display:none">YAY RAELIA!!!! Thank you Pantera for sending me out this beautiful book. The thoughts and opinions in this review are entirely my own. <br /><br />Magic: CHECK. Sarcasm: CHECK. Friendship: HELL YEAH CHECK. <div id="review_1531391442" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1531391442" />
    <a title="Kelly (Diva Booknerd)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11177071-kelly-diva-booknerd"><img alt="Kelly (Diva Booknerd)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1479923328p2/11177071.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1531391442?book_show_action=true">Jan 30, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kelly (Diva Booknerd)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kelly (Diva Booknerd)" href="/user/show/11177071-kelly-diva-booknerd">Kelly (Diva Booknerd)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11177071-kelly-diva-booknerd?shelf=pantera">pantera</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11177071-kelly-diva-booknerd?shelf=loveozya">loveozya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11177071-kelly-diva-booknerd?shelf=middle-grade">middle-grade</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1531391442" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9418650223481045132">4.5 Stars<br/>Raelia is a wonderful edition to The Medoran Chronicles, engaging and delightfully surprising. The storyline resumes shortly after Akarnae, after coming close to losing her freedom at the hands of Aven. Now Alex is back with a vengeance, her training has increased in order to protect the institute and the portal that Aven is so desperate to find.<br/><br/>After the revelations of Akarnae, Alex's character growth was immense. She's always been resilient, but has taken her place at Akarnae in her s</span>
  <span id="freeText9418650223481045132" style="display:none">4.5 Stars<br />Raelia is a wonderful edition to The Medoran Chronicles, engaging and delightfully surprising. The storyline resumes shortly after Akarnae, after coming close to losing her freedom at the hands of Aven. Now Alex is back with a vengeance, her training has increased in order to protect the institute and the portal that Aven is so desperate to find.<br /><br />After the revelations of Akarnae, Alex's character growth was immense. She's always been resilient, but has taken her place at Akarnae in her stride and is relishing in her new found role as a protector of the library and the institution itself. Old characters and friends return. While readers are introduced to new characters in the mystical kingdom of Meya, we now see characters such as the dashing Kaiden and roommate in D.C who is now part of the core character group, with much stronger storylines and interactions with Alex, Bear and Jordan. <br /><br />One of the most appealing aspects of The Medoran Chronicles is the adventure. Comparable to the Harry Potter series, it appeals to young adult and mature middle grade readers as the storyline is morally uncomplicated and doesn't rely on a romance to develop characters or further the storyline which really is a breath of fresh air. I loved the attraction blooming between Kaiden and Alex and hoping the third book explores a potential romance between the two. <br /><br />Once again Lynette Noni's writing is a mixture of sass and humour. The series is perfect for non fantasy reader such as myself as it offers a lighter take on the genre, making it easy for young teens to engage with and relate to it's well written and depth of characters. <br /><br />I love a well written villain and I need more Aven. Aven is mysterious, sinister and delicious. He's single minded in his determination to find the doorway back to Meya, where he is now the exiled prince. I needed him to ignite and his cunning surprised and delighted me, even as villainous as he's portrayed. Be warned, Raelia ends with a heart wrenching revelation. The fate of one character rests upon Alex and her strength to fight.<br /><br />Raelia is an wonderful installment in The Medoran Chronicles. First time author Lynette Noni is a magnificent storyteller, crafting a beautifully written, engaging and enchanting new young adult series with a touch of Australian charm and warmth. <br /><br />My only gripe is that all the characters seem to mumble. Speak clearly children.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9418650223481045132" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText6495169016762066008" style="display:none">I believe that this could be my favourite book in this series. <div id="review_1552009054" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1552009054" />
    <a title="Jeann (Happy Indulgence) " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6186603-jeann-happy-indulgence"><img alt="Jeann (Happy Indulgence) " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1559561558p2/6186603.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jeann (Happy Indulgence) " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jeann (Happy Indulgence) " href="/user/show/6186603-jeann-happy-indulgence">Jeann (Happy Indulgence) </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6186603-jeann-happy-indulgence?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6186603-jeann-happy-indulgence?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6186603-jeann-happy-indulgence?shelf=review-copy">review-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6186603-jeann-happy-indulgence?shelf=love-oz-ya">love-oz-ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6186603-jeann-happy-indulgence?shelf=to-review">to-review</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1552009054" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4801249487560472534">THAT WAS SO FANTASTIC. It's been a few years since I read Akarnae, the first book in the series but everyone's love for this series inspired me to pick up the sequel.<br/><br/>I adored the magical world of Medora with all it's magic and mystic, from the otherworldly Medorans and the detailed combat training of the Akarnae academy. Those fight scenes were so vivid and exhilirating and when there was magic involved, it was even more nail biting. <br/><br/>I also adored Alex, her subtle defiance, her easygoing outlook</span>
  <span id="freeText4801249487560472534" style="display:none">THAT WAS SO FANTASTIC. It's been a few years since I read Akarnae, the first book in the series but everyone's love for this series inspired me to pick up the sequel.<br /><br />I adored the magical world of Medora with all it's magic and mystic, from the otherworldly Medorans and the detailed combat training of the Akarnae academy. Those fight scenes were so vivid and exhilirating and when there was magic involved, it was even more nail biting. <br /><br />I also adored Alex, her subtle defiance, her easygoing outlook on life and the loyalty and banter that she shares with her best friends, DC, Jordan and Bear. Although we didn't really see much of Bear in this one, her other best friends took a primary role in the book which was really wonderful to see. This series really places a focus on platonic friendships and it is so refreshing. <br /><br />The majority of the book focuses on a SAS mission where Alex and her classmates follow subtle clues to achieve their mission objectives and I enjoyed it so much! Loved seeing Alex work with her classmates to go undercover. After the objectives are over though, I kind of found it to be a bit draggy but IT GETS SO GOOD towards the end and I'm still heartbroken.<br /><br />The encounters with the villain Aven were incredibly chilling, as he constantly comes to threaten Alex and her friends. Always love a good ultimate villain and Aven definitely meets that criteria.<br /><br />I also loved seeing more Medorans, Kyria, Rok and Zain were such intriguing, powerful characters and offered a new dimension to the story. My only reservation is Alex's classmate Skyla, her personality was that of a slow airhead and I found the way she was treated to be kind of sad. She really deserves better.<br /><br />Let's not forget the swoony Kaiden who Alex shares a few sweet moments with (some which are completely hilarious). Looking forward to seeing the development of this in coming books!<br /><br />The great thing about getting into a series later is that I don't have to wait until the next book to come out, I can just dive right in. I'm in for the Medoran ride now and I can't wait to read the sequels!</span>
  <a data-text-id="4801249487560472534" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

Yes.<br/><br/>I personally prefer Akarnae, but I think this is a good set up for the next book in the series ;)<br/>________<br/>Actual Rating: 4.25 out of 5 stars<br/><br/>I'm really liking this series so far!   <span id="freeText9031684429466324091" style="display:none">UPDATED REVIEW (reread 2019)<br />I have similar thoughts but taking it down to a solid 4 Stars. Like I said, I do enjoy this book and I do have some critiques. Is it perfect? No. Is it enjoyable though? Yes.<br /><br />I personally prefer Akarnae, but I think this is a good set up for the next book in the series ;)<br />________<br />Actual Rating: 4.25 out of 5 stars<br /><br />I'm really liking this series so far! Just when you think that everything is happy for these characters, it becomes dark all of the sudden. No one is safe. It seriously gave me chills at times.<br /><br />At times I laughed when reading this too... and I may just be shipping Alex and Kaiden a whole lot more &lt;3<br /><br />One thing that really frustrated me was the dialogue from a specific character, and that was Skyla. I understand that she is meant to be a girl-hateish type of character, but her dialogue was kind of written as if she was intended to be a 5 year-old. I wasn't annoyed at her for the character she was supposed to be, rather I was annoyed at how unrealistic how dialogue was for a teen. I don't know why, but I picked up on that for some reason.<br /><br />Other than that, this book was awesome. For some reason, I'm kind of loving Aven. I think that's because I feel like his complexity is unfolding. He makes a great antagonist. The cliff-hanger was unfair though, I mean... why?<br /><br />Can't wait for Draekora!</span>

<div id="review_2746174631" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2746174631" />
    <a title="Brooklyn Tayla" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/34712899-brooklyn-tayla"><img alt="Brooklyn Tayla" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1471946183p2/34712899.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2746174631?book_show_action=true">Aug 28, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brooklyn Tayla" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brooklyn Tayla" href="/user/show/34712899-brooklyn-tayla">Brooklyn Tayla</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34712899-brooklyn-tayla?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34712899-brooklyn-tayla?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34712899-brooklyn-tayla?shelf=my-own-book-collection">my-own-book-collection</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34712899-brooklyn-tayla?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34712899-brooklyn-tayla?shelf=2019-reads">2019-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2746174631" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer276133973947828326">You can also find my review here: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://brooklynthebookworm.wordpress.com/2019/08/29/book-review-raelia-by-lynette-noni/'>https://brooklynthebookworm.wordpress...</a><br/><br/>Raelia is perfection, at every turn! This second instalment in The Medoran Chronicles is every bit as glorious and vast as its predecessor, Lynette Noni has most definitely cemented her place as one of my absolute new favourite authors and I’ve fallen in love with this series with all my heart!<br/>There was never a dull moment in this book, it was every bit as exciting, addictive and enthralling as Akarnae, with so much additi</span>
  <span id="freeText276133973947828326" style="display:none">You can also find my review here: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://brooklynthebookworm.wordpress.com/2019/08/29/book-review-raelia-by-lynette-noni/">https://brooklynthebookworm.wordpress...</a><br /><br />Raelia is perfection, at every turn! This second instalment in The Medoran Chronicles is every bit as glorious and vast as its predecessor, Lynette Noni has most definitely cemented her place as one of my absolute new favourite authors and I’ve fallen in love with this series with all my heart!<br />There was never a dull moment in this book, it was every bit as exciting, addictive and enthralling as Akarnae, with so much additional wonder and awe! It was so amazing reading about the worlds within Medora and all of their features, such as when Alex and her friends find their way into Meya, such a dazzling and breathtaking city! It’s here where our heroes make the acquaintance of some new faces, my favourite being Roka – who indeed is the brother of the villainous Aven! Where Aven is definitely devilishly charming and frankly terrifying (but truly one of my new favourite villains, Roka is inquisitive and curious and caring, truly wanting Alex and her friends to be safe, but knowing that Alex is connected to Aven in ways, and Alex knowing Aven’s plans to reclaim the throne of Meya, just wow!). There was not one moment where I didn’t feel on edge throughout this!<br />There were so many revelations throughout this book, whether its Aven wanting to unleash his fury on Alex and those closest to her (by the end my feelings were a puddle, truly, I did not see the betrayal coming, it just hurt!), but also where there is fear and hurt I know there’s hope, so I definitely am hopeful for a turn around with what one character is now going through! Also though at the same time, I’m kind of looking forward to the darker scenes? Purely though because I’m hopeful that Aven’s deciets and ploys will fail?! Either way, I couldn’t BE more excited to continue my adventure in book 3!<br />I loved all the mystery throughout this book too! Why was Delucia plagued by her nightmares? Were they prophetic or some other kind of darkness? Why was she so weary of Meya? Why was Jordan being so aloof to his very best friends after a weekend with his parents? The ending of this book was equally soul wrenching and satisfying!<br />I have to say though, I admire Alex so much! Whilst she and her classmates are on a quest for one of their classes, I couldn’t help but be in awe of her throughout! She’s so loyal and will stop at nothing to see that her friends are safe, even if that means putting herself in the line of danger! All throughout I was cheering for her and it’s just so great seeing her character develop and embrace her skills and powers! This is the perfect second instalment to a perfect series and I couldn’t put it down! This series is already one of my very favourites and even though I have four books to go and marvel over, I can already see myself rereading them!</span>
  <a data-text-id="276133973947828326" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3567410854" />
    <a title="rose - 忻怡 -" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/116991735-rose----"><img alt="rose - 忻怡 -" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594284498p2/116991735.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="rose - 忻怡 -" class="user" itemprop="url" name="rose - 忻怡 -" href="/user/show/116991735-rose----">rose - 忻怡 -</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">how about everyone?</span></div>

    <span class="greyText">Recommended to rose - 忻怡 - by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/55288713-jamilah">Jamilah</a>

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3567410854" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7885660939672754204"><blockquote>
  <p><b>4.7 stars, loved it loved it loved it ♡</b><br/><br/>Ahhhhh this book has me so hypedddd!!!! The writing is amazing, the language flowing naturally, leading me deeper and deeper into Alex's journey in Medora. In this book, friendship bonds are tested, enemies uncovered, allies found, truths embraced... The plot is full of twists and turns, the conflicts and tension higher than ever. In the magical world of Medora, behind the safe walls of Akarnae, lots unfurl, yet outside, more mysteries present themselves</p></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText7885660939672754204" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <p><b>4.7 stars, loved it loved it loved it ♡</b><br /><br />Ahhhhh this book has me so hypedddd!!!! The writing is amazing, the language flowing naturally, leading me deeper and deeper into Alex's journey in Medora. In this book, friendship bonds are tested, enemies uncovered, allies found, truths embraced... The plot is full of twists and turns, the conflicts and tension higher than ever. In the magical world of Medora, behind the safe walls of Akarnae, lots unfurl, yet outside, more mysteries present themselves.<br /><br />As the author introduced the new characters meticulously, I found myself entranced. On the edge of my seat to learn more about them. Zain. Kyia. Callista. Roka. Hunter. The diverse characters, each one of them beautifully written and their unique personalities clashed together, so different yet carving a big picture of harmony as they fit together impeccably, constructing this magical world.<br /><br />This book is actually deeper than the first. Throughout Alex's voyage, more and more philosophies whirled in my mind, prompting me to digest their complex meanings as the book progressed. Behind the whimsical fantasies, there is so much meaning conveyed by the especially talented author. The Shadow represents darkness of our soul, the evilness and maliciousness that have consumed us all that we are constantly oblivious towards. Raelia - the crossroads. In fact, our lives are packed with them that every step we take, we are choosing the outcome of our life. We are determining our fates ourselves. Almost every concept is a metaphor. One that reflects the author's interesting viewpoint of humankind. There is just so much to read, so much to interpret. So much to digest that every read makes different emotions surface.<br /><br />The only flaw I could find is that the book started off rather plainly. The beginning part of the book couldn't justify its powerful plot. The punchy ending. The fast-paced narrative that had me hooked.<br /><br />But then, it amazed me. Truly. I was shocked, surprised, fascinated, touched, moved... This is seriously, one of the books that I would treasure forever. It made the other books I've read before seem bland. Shallow. Priceless, classic and original, no words could properly describe how in awe I am after reading it. I-I just loved it. So much.</p>
</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="7885660939672754204" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer10037221475421660956">So let's just forget about the ending for a bit while I write this review...<br/>Realia was INCREDIBLE! Completely lived up to my expectations! And yes I read this one day... In fact I really only stopped reading to go to the bathroom and to eat food... But it was worth it! <br/><br/>Although there are only two books so far, The Medoran Chronicles has definitely taken it's place as my favourite series, I just love it so much!   <span id="freeText10037221475421660956" style="display:none">So let's just forget about the ending for a bit while I write this review...<br />Realia was INCREDIBLE! Completely lived up to my expectations! And yes I read this one day... In fact I really only stopped reading to go to the bathroom and to eat food... But it was worth it! <br /><br />Although there are only two books so far, The Medoran Chronicles has definitely taken it's place as my favourite series, I just love it so much! Thank you so incredibly much, Lynette Noni, for bringing this world into my existence through writing. I can't begin to explain the feeling I get toward these books. Definitely my favourite fictional world and comfort books! :)<br /><br />I loved returning to Medora and Akarnae to follow Alex and her friends' adventures. The characters and all their interactions were just as brilliant as they were in Akarnae and so realistic like ahhh. The character development was awesome. I loved Alex's humour/ wit and her strong character. I loved seeing a bit more of D.C. in Raelia and I especially loved all the interactions with Kaiden ;)<br /><br />It was interesting learning more about Alex and Aven and being introduced to 'other characters' who I loved. The whole world is incredibly captivating and getting to explore other places (no spoilers) was really awesome. <br /><br />Overall I thoroughly enjoyed Raelia (and I have to admit that the ending was quite amazing despite my tears *sob*). I need Draekora ASAP but in the meantime I'll just reread the two books and continue to immerse myself in the wonderful world of Medora<br /><br />RECOMMENDED TO EVERYONE (seriously I don't know the amount of times I've told people to read Akarnae)</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7616008105689760207">4.5 <br/>Raelia is the second installment of a 5 part series! That's right 5 books all set in the amazing magical world of Medora. <br/><br/>I love every moment we spend with Alex. Akarnae Academy has an x-man quality to it with all the different classes and lessons, we get to explore a lot more peoples powers and learn more about the Medora race and world. <br/><br/>All of our characters have great relationships and a unique friendship although we don't hear much from Bear in this book but we spend a lot of time with s</span>
  <span id="freeText7616008105689760207" style="display:none">4.5 <br />Raelia is the second installment of a 5 part series! That's right 5 books all set in the amazing magical world of Medora. <br /><br />I love every moment we spend with Alex. Akarnae Academy has an x-man quality to it with all the different classes and lessons, we get to explore a lot more peoples powers and learn more about the Medora race and world. <br /><br />All of our characters have great relationships and a unique friendship although we don't hear much from Bear in this book but we spend a lot of time with some new students and getting to know them was amazing.<br /><br />Alex our main MC is feisty and unable to think before she speaks usually resulting in chuckle worthy mishaps. She makes me groan in embarrassment along side her when she stumbles over her words and laugh at her earth jokes that no one gets!<br /><br />The whole book was well paced and I couldn't put it down, much better then the first so I can only imagine what we have installed for us next.<br /><br />Fantastic ending, no big cliff hanger where there definitely could of been and it was perfectly paced. I can't wait for the next installment!!<br /><br />I'd like to say Thank you to Net galley and Pantera press for allowing me to read this a whole month early! <br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1083703058380364350">As Alex's second year at Arkanae begins things don't go as planned. Somehow she winds up taking part in the trial to enter the mysterious Hunter's Stealth and Subterfuge class, and what is even more crazy is that she passes doing what no other student has ever been able to - complete the trial. <br/><br/>This sets is motion a series of events that leads to Alex and her friends travelling to the lost city of Meya, where she meets the Meyarin Prince, Roka, who is more than willing to help her on her journey</span>
  <span id="freeText1083703058380364350" style="display:none">As Alex's second year at Arkanae begins things don't go as planned. Somehow she winds up taking part in the trial to enter the mysterious Hunter's Stealth and Subterfuge class, and what is even more crazy is that she passes doing what no other student has ever been able to - complete the trial. <br /><br />This sets is motion a series of events that leads to Alex and her friends travelling to the lost city of Meya, where she meets the Meyarin Prince, Roka, who is more than willing to help her on her journey to stopping Aven from returning to the lost city.<br /><br />But things do not go as planned when Alex, on an overnight assignment for her SAS class encounter Aven and those he has under his control.<br /><br />This book wasn't as intoxicating as the first book but it provided a solid continuation to the storyline, which I really enjoyed. The introduction of Meya and the other Meyarins brings another aspect of this world to light and further adds to the intrigue of this place Alex now feels a strong connection with.<br /><br />I look forward to the next book!</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('U5iGUd6RTf5bLKmS281PHoMAE03TEglgDm56cF4HkPrE1wa7yGBzbqz2boQ3hBJ09wM6tUSj7Gewn8QpSwBfWw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('yyMQa78gdDPFFyhrfRBwZieYe+PQEw0nsH18KnbpZZpcbJCBqdFKozLN732RWS0MU5tSG0ei6CAOjMJzY+6qOw==')})
  }
//]]>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer3575788382545170653">Lynette Noni studied journalism and academic writing at university before completing a degree in human behavior. She lives on the Sunshine Coast in Australia and can be found baking cupcakes, singing along to animated movies, or daydreaming about being swept away to a fantasy world. Some days, she can even do all three at once — and still find the time to sneak in a nap afterwards. </span>
